 train main mahilaon ke liye rigerv bogi main kisi bhi purush yatri kaa ghusna aparaadh he
 If a woman enters a bogie, she can be fined
 saath hi titii aise purush yatri ko bogi se nikaal saktaa he
 2
 railway act kii dhara 156 ke tahat train kii chat, sidhiyon, daravaajon or ingine main baithkar yatra karne par teen maheene kii jail ho sakati he
 Also, a fine can be imposed
 3
 According to Section 167 of the Railway Act, smoking in a train is a crime
 aise logon par jurmaana lagaaya ja saktaa he
 4
 agar yatra ke dauraan yaa yatra khatm hone ke baad titii tikat dikhaane ko kahata he, to yatri ko tikat dikhaanaa hoga
 If not done then action can be taken against that passenger
 5
 No one is allowed to travel on the train by drinking or intoxicating and abusing
 aisa karne vaale ko train se utaarne ke saath hi uske khilaaf railway act kii dhara 145 ke tahat karrwai kii ja sakati he
 In such a case a provision of 6 months jail and fine has been made
 6
 Under section 141 of the Railway Act, it is also a crime to drive a train or beg
 aisa karne vaale ko ek saal kii jail kii sajaa ho sakati he
 May also have to pay a fine
 7
 No one has the right to sell the train ticket without the permission of the railway
 agar koi tikat bechate pakadaa jaataa he, to uske khilaaf railway act kii dhara 142 ke tahat karrwai kii ja sakati he
 In such a case a provision of three months jail and fine has been made
 8
 Stoning in a train is a serious crime
 aisa karne par railway act kii dhara 150 ke tahat 10 saal kii jail kii sajaa or jurmaane kaa praavdhaan kiya gaya he
 9
 railway act kii dhara 151 ke tahat train main aagjanee karne yaa train ko nuksaan pahunchane par 5 saal kii jail ho sakati he
 Can also be fined
 10
 According to the Railway Act, if a person is suffering from an infection disease, he will have to take special permission of the railway to travel on the train
 agar aisa marij bina ijaajat liye yatra karata he, to usko train se utaara ja saktaa he
 Not only this, hitchhikers traveling with such patients can also be taken off the train
 saath hi uskaa tikat bhi jabt kiya ja saktaa he

 ham aapako kuch tips bataa rahe hai jinaki madad se aap apni dosti ko behatar bana sakate hai
 If you want to maintain your friendship for life, then keep these things in mind
 
 
 1
 Don't just run your self, everyone needs friends who are with you
 aise nahin jo bos kii tarah vyavhaar karen
 Therefore, in a friendship relationship, never just run yourselves, but also listen to your friends and try to understand their point
 2
 Do not make fun of friends on the talk, there are laughs and jokes among the friends, but avoid making fun of your friends on the talk
 doston kaa kaam ek-duusare ko saport karnaa hota he na kii ek-duusare ko nicha dikhaanaa
 Doing this can cause a rift in your friendship
 Friendship Day 2018: doston ko den ye sehat kaa uphaar3
 Give time to friends
 We all have our important tasks, but a true friend definitely comes to support in times of need
 agar aap jarurat ke samay bhi doston se apane biji hone kii baat kahenge to aap ek achche dost nahin ban paaegein, kyonki jo dost jarurat ke samay kaam nahin aa saktaa vah kabhi acha dost nahin ban saktaa
 4
 doston se maafee maangane se hichkichaayen nahingalati kisi se bhi ho sakati he or apni galati ko maan lene main hi samajhadaari hoti he
 If your friend gets angry with you due to some mistake, do not hesitate to apologize to your friend
 apane dost ko apane dil kii baat bataaen ki aap unke bina kaisaa mahasoos kar rahe hai
 By doing this your friendship relationship will be stronger than before
 5
 Never make friends by means There are some people who remember their friends only when they are mean or when they are working

 Upset about not getting a wicket in this match, Mohammad Aamir started messing up from the pitch
 gend phenkane ke baad aamir baar-baar pich par aa rahe the
 The bowler is not allowed to enter the Danger Zone of the pitch in the middle of the wicket, but Mohammad Aamir was warned in the third over only by the umpire rebuking it
